```diff
 parse = "(?P<major>\\d+)\\.(?P<minor>\\d+)\\.(?P<patch>\\d+)(\\.(?P<release>[a-z]+)(?P<dev>\\d+))?"
 serialize = ["{major}.{minor}.{patch}"]
```
